I think this is a very good embodiment of the quality of hotel operationüëç

1) Breakfast can be richer, if not, it is recommended to lower the charge for minors over 1.4 meters;
2) The cooling effect of the air conditioner in my room is not very good;
3) In the indoor swimming pool, I didn't see any staff on duty outside the pool during the hour I was swimming. Although the water depth is only 1.2M, there must still be a special lifeguard present. It is very likely that the child is alone in the water while the parents are playing with mobile phones in the rest area on the shore, not paying attention to the dangerous situation;
4) The Biluochun tea served in the room, I didn‚Äôt drink the black tea, but the green tea felt too bitter. Maybe it‚Äôs because the tea set is relatively small and the concentration is too high? Need to optimize;
5) The gate of Taimeiyi County is still relatively low-key. It is recommended to discuss with the road administrator whether it is possible to add a sign on the road outside the gate, otherwise it is easy to miss the hotel gate without braking in time;
In short, for a hotel connoisseur like me, it was a very satisfying stay. I give it a five-star praise and strongly recommend it!
